## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x010D [0x37] UPDATE_EVENT_POSITION_AND_DIR: x=-67.741*, z=-7.751*, y=-9.250*, direction=17.8*
  1: 0x0116 [0x80] LOAD_WAIT(entity=EventEntity)
  2: 0x011B [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
